processing of personal data and on the free movement of such data, and repealing Directive 95/46/EC (General Data Protection Regulation - GDPR).\r\n\r\nThe application can be used as a stand-alone solution or as part of the enterprise cyber protection system  (system BS-1421R).\r\n\r\n\r\nCUSTOMIZABLE AND EASY\r\n\r\nWorking with FPS does not require special knowledge.
